 START_ARTIST Kanye West ::: Chicago, IL, United States ::: 
                Kanye Omari West (born June 8, 1977 in Atlanta, Georgia) is a Grammy award winning rapper, producer, author, designer and singer.   He began making beats and rapping in the early 90s in Chicago, IL, United States when he formed the rap group <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Go+Getters" class="bbcode_artist">Go Getters</a> with Chicago natives <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/GLC" class="bbcode_artist">GLC</a> and <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Really+Doe" class="bbcode_artist">Really Doe</a>. He later gained nationwide popularity in New York when he began producing tracks for artists such as <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Jay-Z" class="bbcode_artist">Jay-Z</a>, <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Twista" class="bbcode_artist">Twista</a>, <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Mase" class="bbcode_artist">Mase</a>, <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Talib+Kweli" class="bbcode_artist">Talib Kweli</a> and <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Alicia+Keys" class="bbcode_artist">Alicia Keys</a>.   

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Kanye+West">Read more about Kanye West on Last.fm</a>.

 START_ARTIST Lana Del Rey ::: Lake Placid, New York, United States ::: 
                Elizabeth &quot;Lizzy&quot; Grant (born 21 June 1986), better known as Lana Del Rey, is a <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/singer-songwriter" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">singer-songwriter</a> from Lake Placid, New York, United States.  Del Rey is known for embellishing her songs and music videos with an eerily nostalgic vibe heavy on Americana themes, including images of surfing, Coney Island, Frank Sinatra, and Marilyn Monroe.  START_ARTIST Arctic Monkeys ::: Sheffield, South Yorkshire, England ::: 
                Arctic Monkeys are an <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/indie%20rock" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">indie rock</a> band formed in Sheffield, South Yorkshire, England in 2002 after meeting at Stocksbridge High School. The band consists of <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Alex+Turner" class="bbcode_artist">Alex Turner</a> (vocals, guitar), <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Jamie+Cook" class="bbcode_artist">Jamie Cook</a> (guitar), <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Nick+O%27Malley" class="bbcode_artist">Nick O'Malley</a> (bass) and <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Matt+Helders" class="bbcode_artist">Matt Helders</a> (drums, vocals). Founding bassist <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Andy+Nicholson" class="bbcode_artist">Andy Nicholson</a> left in 2006.  The band has released four studio albums, &quot;Whatever People Say I Am, That's What I'm Not&quot; (2006), &quot;Favourite Worst Nightmare&quot; (2007), &quot;Humbug&quot; (2009) and &quot;Suck It and See&quot; (2011), all of which debuted at #1 on the UK Albums Chart. Their fifth, &quot;AM&quot;, will be released on 9 September 2013.

 START_ARTIST Coldplay ::: London, United Kingdom ::: 
                Coldplay is a British <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/alternative%20rock" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">alternative rock</a> band, formed in London, United Kingdom in 1997. The band comprises vocalist and pianist <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Chris+Martin" class="bbcode_artist">Chris Martin</a>, lead guitarist <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Jonny+Buckland" class="bbcode_artist">Jonny Buckland</a>, bassist <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Guy+Berryman" class="bbcode_artist">Guy Berryman</a>, and drummer <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Will+Champion" class="bbcode_artist">Will Champion</a>.  Having released four successful albums, (all of which debuted at #1 on the UK album chart) Coldplay have also achieved great success with their singles, such as <a title="Coldplay &ndash; Yellow" href="http://www.last.fm/music/Coldplay/_/Yellow" class="bbcode_track">Yellow</a>, <a title="Coldplay &ndash; Speed of Sound" href="http://www.last.fm/music/Coldplay/_/Speed+of+Sound" class="bbcode_track">Speed of Sound</a>, the Grammy-winning <a title="Coldplay &ndash; Clocks" href="http://www.last.fm/music/Coldplay/_/Clocks" class="bbcode_track">Clocks</a> and the US and UK #1 single <a title="Coldplay &ndash; Viva la Vida" href="http://www.last.fm/music/Coldplay/_/Viva+la+Vida" class="bbcode_track">Viva la Vida</a>.  Frontman Chris Martin credits 1980s Norwegian pop band <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/a-ha" class="bbcode_artist">a-ha</a> for inspiring him to form his own band. 

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Coldplay">Read more about Coldplay on Last.fm</a>.

 START_ARTIST Daft Punk ::: Paris, France ::: 
                Daft Punk is a multi Grammy Award-winning <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/electronic" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">electronic</a> music duo formed in 1994 in Paris, France, and consisting of <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/french">French</a> musicians <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Thomas+Bangalter" class="bbcode_artist">Thomas Bangalter</a> (born 3 January 1975) and <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Guy-Manuel+de+Homem-Christo" class="bbcode_artist">Guy-Manuel de Homem-Christo</a> (born 8 February 1974). The band is considered one of the most successful electronic music collaborations of all time, both in album sales and in critical acclaim.   Daft Punk reached significant popularity in the late <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/90s" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">90s</a> <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/house" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">house</a> movement in <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/france">France</a>, along with other artists such as <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Air" class="bbcode_artist">Air</a>, <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Cassius" class="bbcode_artist">Cassius</a>, and <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Dimitri+from+Paris" class="bbcode_artist">Dimitri from Paris</a>.

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Daft+Punk">Read more about Daft Punk on Last.fm</a>.

 START_ARTIST Radiohead ::: Abingdon, Oxfordshire, United Kingdom ::: 
                Radiohead are an English alternative rock band from Abingdon, Oxfordshire. The band is composed of Thom Yorke (lead vocals, rhythm guitar, piano, beats), Jonny Greenwood (lead guitar, keyboard, other instruments), Ed O'Brien (guitar, backing vocals), Colin Greenwood (bass guitar) and Phil Selway (drums, percussion).  Radiohead released their first single, &quot;Creep,&quot; in 1992. The song was initially unsuccessful, but it became a worldwide hit several months after the release of their debut album, Pablo Honey (1993).

Macklemore's gift, like that of all great songwriters, is his ability to speak on universal experiences in a uniquely personal way.

 START_ARTIST Calvin Harris ::: Dumfries, Scotland ::: 
                Calvin Harris (born 17 January 1984), is a Scottish singer, songwriter and record producer. He was born and grew up in Dumfries, Scotland. His interest in electronic music surfaced in his early teenage years, producing his first bedroom demo by the age of 15.   His first album <a title="Calvin Harris - I Created Disco" href="http://www.last.fm/music/Calvin+Harris/I+Created+Disco" class="bbcode_album">I Created Disco</a> was released on 18 June 2007. The album contained up-tempo <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/electroclash" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">electroclash</a> songs that were influenced by music from the 1980s. To promote 'I Created Disco', Harris embarked on a tour of the UK, supporting <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Faithless" class="bbcode_artist">Faithless</a> and <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Groove+Armada" class="bbcode_artist">Groove Armada</a>.

 START_ARTIST Justin Timberlake ::: Memphis, Tennessee ::: 
                Justin Randall Timberlake (born January 31, 1981 in Memphis, Tennessee) is a Grammy Award winning singer, Emmy Award winning actor, producer and dancer.   At a young age of 4, Timberlake already had a love for music. Joining singing competitions as early as age 7, he was coached by well-renowned child coach Bob Westbrook. After an appearance on Star Search, he continued his dreams, beating out thousands of kids to join the cast of Disney's Mickey Mouse Club. At age 15, he rose to commercial fame as one of the frontmen of the hugely successful pop group <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/*NSYNC" class="bbcode_artist">*NSYNC</a> in the late 90's.

 START_ARTIST Linkin Park ::: Agoura Hills, California ::: 
                Linkin Park is an American band from Agoura Hills, California. Formed in 1996, the band rose to international fame with their debut album, Hybrid Theory, which was certified Diamond by the RIAA in 2005 and multi-platinum in several other countries. Its following studio album, Meteora, continued the band's success, topping the Billboard 200 album chart in 2003, and was followed by extensive touring and charity work around the world. In 2003, MTV2 named Linkin Park the sixth greatest band of the music video era and the third best of the new millennium behind <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Oasis" class="bbcode_artist">Oasis</a> and <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Coldplay" class="bbcode_artist">Coldplay</a>.

Pink Floyd is one of <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/rock" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">rock</a>'s most successful and influential acts, having sold over 200 million albums worldwide and with 74.5 million certified units in the United States, making them one of the best-selling artists of all time.  START_ARTIST Queens of the Stone Age ::: Palm Desert, California, United States :::

The band is frequently labeled <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/stoner%20rock" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">stoner rock</a>, although they reject the label. They developed a style of riff-oriented, heavy music which the band's founder and mastermind <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Josh+Homme" class="bbcode_artist">Josh Homme</a> described as &quot;<a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/robot%20rock" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">robot rock</a>&quot;, saying that he &quot;wanted to create a heavy sound based on a solid jam, just pound it into your head&quot;. Since then, their sound has evolved to incorporate a variety of different styles and influences.

The Black Keys have roots in traditional blues and <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/psychedelic%20rock" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">psychedelic rock</a> stylings.

 START_ARTIST David Guetta ::: Paris ::: 
                David Guetta (born November 7th, 1967 in Paris) is a French DJ.  He was the pioneer of French house with &quot;<a title="David Guetta &ndash; Up &amp; away" href="http://www.last.fm/music/David+Guetta/_/Up+&amp;+away" class="bbcode_track">Up &amp; away</a>,&quot; a garage-style track with vocals by <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Robert+Owens" class="bbcode_artist">Robert Owens</a> released in 1994 – really made a name for himself in the mid-90s as one of the key catalysts of Parisian nightlife by promoting evenings at such renowned Paris hot spots as Folies Pigalle, Queen, Bataclan, Palace and Les Bains, where he invited DJ legends like Little Louie Vega, David Morales, DJ Pierre and Roger Sanchez to join him on the turntables. In 2001, however, he went back to his first love: making music. 

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/David+Guetta">Read more about David Guetta on Last.fm</a>.
    
     END_ARTIST

 START_ARTIST Queen ::: London ::: 
                Queen were an English rock band originally consisting of four members: vocalist <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Freddie+Mercury" class="bbcode_artist">Freddie Mercury</a>, guitarist <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Brian+May" class="bbcode_artist">Brian May</a>, bass guitarist <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/John+Deacon" class="bbcode_artist">John Deacon</a>, and drummer <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Roger+Taylor" class="bbcode_artist">Roger Taylor</a>.  The band formed in London in 1970 after May and Taylor's former band <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Smile" class="bbcode_artist">Smile</a> split after having released an album and single. Freddie replaced lead vocalist <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Tim+Staffell" class="bbcode_artist">Tim Staffell</a>, after the latter's departure from the original trio.   There was much deliberation as to what the band's name would be. May and Taylor had settled upon the Grand Dance, derived from a C.S. Lewis Trilogy of books Out Of The Silent Planet.

 START_ARTIST Green Day :::  East Bay, CA, United States  ::: 
                Green Day is an American rock trio formed in 1987. The band has consisted of Billie Joe Armstrong (vocals, guitar), Mike Dirnt (bass guitar, vocals), and Tré Cool (drums, percussion) for the majority of its existence.  Green Day was originally part of the punk rock scene at 924 Gilman Street, Berkeley in  East Bay, CA, United States . Its early releases for independent record label Lookout! Records earned them a grassroots fanbase, some of whom felt alienated when the band signed to a major label.

 START_ARTIST Black Sabbath ::: Birmingham, West Midlands, England, United Kingdom ::: 
                Black Sabbath is an English <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/heavy%20metal" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">heavy metal</a> band formed in 1968 in Birmingham, West Midlands, England, United Kingdom, originally comprising <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Ozzy+Osbourne" class="bbcode_artist">Ozzy Osbourne</a> (vocals), <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Tony+Iommi" class="bbcode_artist">Tony Iommi</a> (guitar), <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Geezer+Butler" class="bbcode_artist">Geezer Butler</a> (bass), and <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Bill+Ward" class="bbcode_artist">Bill Ward</a> (drums). In the early 1970s they were the first to pair heavily distorted, sonically dissonant blues-rock at slow speeds with lyrics about drugs, mental pain, and abominations of war, thus giving birth to generations of metal bands that followed in their wake. They are often credited with creating the <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/heavy%20metal" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">heavy metal</a> genre as well as the <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/doom%20metal" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">doom metal</a> subgenre. 

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Black+Sabbath">Read more about Black Sabbath on Last.fm</a>.

 START_ARTIST Icona Pop ::: Stockholm, Sweden ::: 
                Icona Pop is a duo from Stockholm, Sweden. Caroline Hjelt and Aino Jawo deliver pop music that seems second nature to most Scandinavians.  Upon first hearing Manners you get it all – clapped beats, fizzy electronics, cute female vocals and a Sesame Street chorus. It’s verses are like the narration of a teenager’s diary, before the youthful confidence comes storming in, “take a second look and you’ll see, there is no one like me“. It’s a punchy pop song that has a wonderful blend of obvious hooks, big choruses and a chart-ready appeal, yet it’s still drenched in buckets of ice cool undertones.

 START_ARTIST The Offspring ::: Huntington Beach, California, United States ::: 
                The Offspring is a punk rock band formed in Huntington Beach, California, United States in 1984. Since its formation, the band's line-up had included Dexter Holland (lead vocals, guitar), Noodles (lead and rhythm guitars, back vocals), Greg K. (bass, back vocals), and Ron Welty (drums, percussion), who left in 2003. Their current drummer is Pete Parada, formerly of <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Face+to+Face" class="bbcode_artist">Face to Face</a> and <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Saves+The+Day" class="bbcode_artist">Saves The Day</a>, who has been with the band since 2007.

To date, The Offspring has released eight studio albums, one compilation, four EPs and three DVDs. They have sold over 34 million albums worldwide, making them one of the best-selling punk rock acts of all time. Each album since the release of their 1994 album Smash has sold over a million units.

The band consisted of <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Jim+Morrison" class="bbcode_artist">Jim Morrison</a> (vocals), <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Ray+Manzarek" class="bbcode_artist">Ray Manzarek</a> (organ), <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Robby+Krieger" class="bbcode_artist">Robby Krieger</a> (guitar) and <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/John+Densmore" class="bbcode_artist">John Densmore</a> (drums). In this configuration, the band released six albums, all of which were successful and reached #1 on the Billboard Hot 100 twice, with 1967's &quot;Light My Fire&quot; and 1968's &quot;Hello, I Love You&quot;.  After Morrison's death in 1971, the band continued on as a trio, releasing two more albums that were ignored commercially and disliked critically before disbanding in 1973.

The two most successful periods for the band were during the late 19<a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/60s" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">60s</a> British <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/blues" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">blues</a> boom, when they were led by guitarist <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Peter+Green" class="bbcode_artist">Peter Green</a>; and from 1975-87, with more <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/pop" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">pop</a>-orientation, featuring <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Christine+McVie" class="bbcode_artist">Christine McVie</a>, <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Lindsey+Buckingham" class="bbcode_artist">Lindsey Buckingham</a> and <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Stevie+Nicks" class="bbcode_artist">Stevie Nicks</a>.

 START_ARTIST Lykke Li ::: Stockholm ::: 
                Lykke Li (born Li Lykke Timotej Svensson Zachrisson on 18 March 1986 in Ystad, Sweden) is a Swedish singer-songwriter. Her music often blends elements of pop, indie rock and electronic; various instruments can also be found in her songs, including violins, synthesizers, tambourines, trumpets, saxophones and cellos. Li possesses the vocal range of a soprano.  Li was raised by artistic parents (her mother was a photographer, her father is a musician). As a toddler the family moved to Stockholm. They have released a number of works, most notably the studio albums <a title="Boards of Canada - Music Has the Right to Children" href="http://www.last.fm/music/Boards+of+Canada/Music+Has+the+Right+to+Children" class="bbcode_album">Music Has the Right to Children</a> (1998), <a title="Boards of Canada - Geogaddi" href="http://www.last.fm/music/Boards+of+Canada/Geogaddi" class="bbcode_album">Geogaddi</a> (2002), and <a title="Boards of Canada - The Campfire Headphase" href="http://www.last.fm/music/Boards+of+Canada/The+Campfire+Headphase" class="bbcode_album">The Campfire Headphase</a> (2005) on the pioneering electronic music label <a href="http://www.last.fm/label/Warp" class="bbcode_label">Warp</a>. Their fourth album <a title="Boards of Canada - Tomorrow's Harvest" href="http://www.last.fm/music/Boards+of+Canada/Tomorrow%27s+Harvest" class="bbcode_album">Tomorrow's Harvest</a> was released in June 2013.  

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Boards+of+Canada">Read more about Boards of Canada on Last.fm</a>.
    
     END_ARTIST
 START_ARTIST Jack Johnson ::: North Shore, Oahu, Hawaii ::: 
                Jack Hody Johnson (born May 18, 1975 in North Shore, Oahu, Hawaii) is a singer-songwriter, accomplished professional surfer and filmmaker who has achieved critical and commercial success and a dedicated following since he first appeared on <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/G.+Love+&amp;+Special+Sauce" class="bbcode_artist">G. Love &amp; Special Sauce</a>'s album Philadelphonic. The release of his 2001 debut album, Brushfire Fairytales, further cemented his popularity and he has since released four more successful albums including 2003's On and On, 2005's In Between Dreams, 2008's Sleep Through the Static and 2010's To The Sea.

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Jack+Johnson">Read more about Jack Johnson on Last.fm</a>.
    
     END_ARTIST
 START_ARTIST Portishead ::: Bristol, United Kingdom ::: 
                Portishead are a band from Bristol, United Kingdom, named after a small coastal town twelve miles west of said musical hotbed, in North Somerset. They were initially known for their use of <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/jazz" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">jazz</a> samples and some <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/hip-hop" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">hip-hop</a> beats along with various synth sounds and the hauntingly beautiful vocals of singer Beth Gibbons. Their current sound drops the samples in favour of a harder, more abrasive edge, but retains Gibbons' vocals.  

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Portishead">Read more about Portishead on Last.fm</a>.
    
     END_ARTIST
 START_ARTIST Regina Spektor ::: New York, United States ::: 
                Regina Spektor (born Regina Ilyinichna Spektor on 18 February 1980 in Moscow) is a Russian-born American singer-songwriter and pianist. Her music is associated with the anti-folk scene centered on New York City's East Village.  Spektor studied classical piano from the age of six, practising on a Petrof piano given to her mother by her grandfather. She was also exposed to the music of rock and roll bands such as <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/The+Beatles" class="bbcode_artist">The Beatles</a>, <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Queen" class="bbcode_artist">Queen</a>, and <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/The+Moody+Blues" class="bbcode_artist">The Moody Blues</a> by her father, who obtained such recordings in Eastern Europe and traded cassettes with friends in the Soviet Union.

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Regina+Spektor">Read more about Regina Spektor on Last.fm</a>.
    
     END_ARTIST
 START_ARTIST Beastie Boys ::: New York City, United States ::: 
                Beastie Boys are an American <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/hip-hop" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">hip-hop</a> trio from New York City, United States: Brooklyn and Manhattan. The members are <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Mike+D" class="bbcode_artist">Mike D</a> (real name Michael Diamond),  <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Ad-Rock" class="bbcode_artist">Ad-Rock</a> (Adam Horovitz) and, until his death in May 2012, <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/MCA" class="bbcode_artist">MCA</a> (Adam Yauch).  The Beastie Boys were the first successful white rap group and one of the few acts from the early days of hip-hop that still enjoy major success. Their rock and punk-influenced rap has had a significant impact on artists both in and outside the hip-hop scene, and they were the first rap group to gain a substantial following with <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/alternative%20rock" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">alternative rock</a> fans. 

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Beastie+Boys">Read more about Beastie Boys on Last.fm</a>.
    
     END_ARTIST
 START_ARTIST Kelly Clarkson ::: Fort Worth, TX ::: 
                <a href="http://www.kellyofficial.com" rel="nofollow">Kelly Brianne Clarkson</a> (born April 24, 1982 in Fort Worth, TX) is a Grammy-winning American <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/singer-songwriter" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">singer-songwriter</a> and occasional actress. Clarkson recorded her debut album with RCA Records after having won the highly-publicized first season of the television series American Idol in 2002.   Though originally marketed as a <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/pop" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">pop</a> musician, she eventually developed a more <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/rock" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">rock</a>-oriented image. Her debut album, <a title="Kelly Clarkson - Thankful" href="http://www.last.fm/music/Kelly+Clarkson/Thankful" class="bbcode_album">Thankful</a>, was released in 2003 and debuted at #1 on the Billboard 200 with almost 300,000 copies sold in its first week.

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Kelly+Clarkson">Read more about Kelly Clarkson on Last.fm</a>.

 START_ARTIST Björk ::: Reykjavík, Iceland :::

She is known for including elements of <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/rock" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">rock</a>, <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/jazz" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">jazz</a>, <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/electronic" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">electronic</a>, <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/classical" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">classical</a>, <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/industrial" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">industrial</a>, <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/folk" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">folk</a> and <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/trip-hop" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">trip-hop</a> music in her work. Her voice has also been acclaimed for its distinctive qualities. She is also known for her eccentric costumes and music videos.  START_ARTIST Grimes ::: Montreal, Canada ::: 
                Grimes is the alias of the <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/electronic" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">electronic</a> musician Claire Boucher (born in 17 March 1988 in Vancouver, Canada and based in Montreal). Her music is an eclectic mix of styles which she described herself as &quot;ADD music&quot;, because it shifts frequently and dramatically. She fuses contemporary instrumentation with classical vocal practices.  Boucher was born and raised in Vancouver, British Columbia. She graduated from Lord Byng Secondary School and studied ballet for 11 years.

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Grimes">Read more about Grimes on Last.fm</a>.

 START_ARTIST Flo Rida ::: Miami, Florida ::: 
                Tramar Dillard (born September 17, 1979 in Miami, Florida), better known by his stage name Flo Rida, is an American rapper signed to Poe Boy Entertainment. He began his rap career touring with <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/2+Live+Crew" class="bbcode_artist">2 Live Crew</a> and was then featured on <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/DJ+Khaled" class="bbcode_artist">DJ Khaled</a>'s album &quot;We The Best&quot; in 2006. He released his debut album Mail on Sunday in 2008 and it's lead single, Low featuring <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/T-Pain" class="bbcode_artist">T-Pain</a>, held a run of 10 weeks at #1 on the Billboard Hot 100. In 2009, he released his second album R.O.O.T.S, and its first single, Right Round featuring <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Ke$ha" class="bbcode_artist">Ke$ha</a>, was #1 for six weeks.

 START_ARTIST Röyksopp ::: Tromsø, Norway ::: 
                Röyksopp is an <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/electronic" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">electronic</a> music duo formed in 1998 in Tromsø, Norway and currently based in Bergen, Norway. The band consists of Torbjørn Brundtland and Svein Berge, both being songwriters, producers and remixers.  START_ARTIST Alicia Keys ::: New York City, New York, United States ::: 
                Alicia Augello Cook (born January 25, 1981), better known by her stage name Alicia Keys, is an American recording artist, musician and actress. She was raised by a single mother in the Hell's Kitchen area of Manhattan in New York City, New York, United States. At age seven, Keys began to play classical music on the piano. She attended Professional Performing Arts School and graduated at 16 as valedictorian. She later attended Columbia University before dropping out to pursue her music career.

 START_ARTIST The Knife ::: Stockholm, Sweden :::

The group rarely makes public appearances, most of their promotional photos feature the members wearing masks, and formerly refused to perform live concerts.  START_ARTIST Outkast ::: Atlanta, Georgia, United States ::: 
                Outkast is an American <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/hip-hop" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">hip-hop</a> duo from Atlanta, Georgia, United States.  The duo is one of the most successful hip-hop groups of all time, having received six Grammy Awards.   Over 25 million copies have been sold of Outkast's seven releases: six studio albums—including one double album—and a greatest hits release.   The group's original musical style was a mixture of Dirty South and G-Funk.  Since then funk, soul, pop, electronic music, rock, spoken word poetry, jazz, and blues have been added to the group's musical palette.

 START_ARTIST Elton John ::: Pinner, Middlesex, England :::

 START_ARTIST Neil Young ::: Toronto ::: 
                Neil Percival Young (born November 12, 1945) is a Canadian singer-songwriter who is widely regarded as one of the most influential musicians of his generation. Young was born in Toronto, but moved to the family home of Winnipeg as a child, which is where his music career began. Young began performing as a solo artist in Canada in 1960, before moving to California in 1966, where he co-founded the band <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Buffalo+Springfield" class="bbcode_artist">Buffalo Springfield</a> along with <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Stephen+Stills" class="bbcode_artist">Stephen Stills</a> and <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Richie+Furay" class="bbcode_artist">Richie Furay</a>, and later joined <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Crosby,+Stills+&amp;+Nash" class="bbcode_artist">Crosby, Stills &amp; Nash</a> as a fourth member in 1969 (forming <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Crosby,+Stills,+Nash+&amp;+Young" class="bbcode_artist">Crosby, Stills, Nash &amp; Young</a>).

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Neil+Young">Read more about Neil Young on Last.fm</a>.

 START_ARTIST Dire Straits ::: Newcastle, United Kingdom ::: 
                Dire Straits were a <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/british" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">british</a> <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/rock" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">rock</a> band from Newcastle, United Kingdom,  formed in 1977 by <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Mark+Knopfler" class="bbcode_artist">Mark Knopfler</a> (guitar and vocals), his brother <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/David+Knopfler" class="bbcode_artist">David Knopfler</a> (guitar), <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/John+Illsley" class="bbcode_artist">John Illsley</a> (bass), and <span title="Unknown artist" class="bbcode_unknown">Pick Withers</span> (drums), and subsequently managed by Ed Bicknell. Dire Straits emerged during the <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/post-punk" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">post-punk</a> era of the late '70s, and while their sound was minimalistic and stripped down, they owed little to <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/punk" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">punk</a>. If anything, the band was a direct outgrowth of the roots revivalism of <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/pub%20rock" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">pub rock</a>, but where pub rock celebrated good times, Dire Straits were melancholy.

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Dire+Straits">Read more about Dire Straits on Last.fm</a>.

                Deep Purple is an English <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/rock" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">rock</a> band formed in Hertfordshire in 1968. Together with <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Led+Zeppelin" class="bbcode_artist">Led Zeppelin</a> and <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Black+Sabbath" class="bbcode_artist">Black Sabbath</a> they are considered to be heavy metal pioneers. Especially influential to heavy metal were <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Ian+Gillan" class="bbcode_artist">Ian Gillan</a>'s powerful screams and <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Ritchie+Blackmore" class="bbcode_artist">Ritchie Blackmore</a>'s virtuoso solos.  Deep Purple were also very influential to <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/progressive%20rock" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">progressive rock</a>.  Deep Purple's early output ranged from rock (such as their cover of <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Joe+South" class="bbcode_artist">Joe South</a>'s &quot;<a title="Deep Purple &ndash; Hush" href="http://www.last.fm/music/Deep+Purple/_/Hush" class="bbcode_track">Hush</a>)&quot; to strongly classically influenced pieces (such as &quot;<a title="Deep Purple &ndash; April" href="http://www.last.fm/music/Deep+Purple/_/April" class="bbcode_track">April</a>&quot;, from their third album).

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Deep+Purple">Read more about Deep Purple on Last.fm</a>.
    
     END_ARTIST

 START_ARTIST Stevie Wonder ::: Saginaw, Michigan ::: 
                Stevland Hardaway Morris (born on May 13, 1950 in Saginaw, Michigan), known by his stage name Stevie Wonder, is a U.S. singer-songwriter, multi-instrumentalist, record producer, and activist.   Born as Stevland Hardaway Judkins, he lost his sight shortly after birth.  When Wonder was four, his mother left his father and moved herself and her children to Detroit. She changed her name back to Lula Hardaway and later changed her son's surname to Morris, partly because of relatives. Morris has remained Stevie Wonder's legal name ever since.

 START_ARTIST The Velvet Underground ::: New York City ::: 
                The Velvet Underground was a pioneering <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/experimental%20rock" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">experimental rock</a> band from New York City first active from 1965 to 1973. Its best-known lineup consisted of vocalist/guitarist <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Lou+Reed" class="bbcode_artist">Lou Reed</a>, bassist/violist <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/John+Cale" class="bbcode_artist">John Cale</a>, guitarist <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Sterling+Morrison" class="bbcode_artist">Sterling Morrison</a> and drummer <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/+noredirect/Maureen+Tucker" class="bbcode_artist">Maureen Tucker</a>. The band also collaborated with <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Nico" class="bbcode_artist">Nico</a> for their debut album in 1967, under the supervision of producer and pop artist Andy Warhol.  Some see The Velvet Underground as being a bridge between the pacifist themes of the late 60s and the sheer chaos and indifference of the mid-70s <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/punk" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">punk</a> movement.

 START_ARTIST Ramones ::: Queens, New York, United States ::: 
                The Ramones were a <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/punk%20rock" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">punk rock</a> band that formed in Queens, New York, United States, in 1974. They are often cited as the first punk group. Despite achieving only limited commercial success, the band was a major influence on the punk rock movement both in the United States and the United Kingdom.  All of the band members adopted pseudonyms ending with the surname &quot;Ramone&quot;, though none of them were related. They performed 2,263 concerts, touring virtually nonstop for 22 years. In 1996, after a tour with the Lollapalooza music festival, the band played a farewell concert and disbanded.

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Ramones">Read more about Ramones on Last.fm</a>.

Murdoch has a gift not only for whimsy and surrealism, but also for odd, unsettling lyrical detail which keeps the songs grounded in a tangible reality. Waits is often compared to Charles Bukowski, being similar both in content and lifestyle, although Waits's views are more egalitarian than Bukowski's.

 START_ARTIST The Jimi Hendrix Experience ::: London ::: 
                The Jimi Hendrix Experience was a short-lived, yet highly influential rock band famous for the guitar work of <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Jimi+Hendrix" class="bbcode_artist">Jimi Hendrix</a> (1942– 1970) on songs such as <a title="The Jimi Hendrix Experience &ndash; Purple Haze" href="http://www.last.fm/music/The+Jimi+Hendrix+Experience/_/Purple+Haze" class="bbcode_track">Purple Haze</a>, <a title="The Jimi Hendrix Experience &ndash; Foxy Lady" href="http://www.last.fm/music/The+Jimi+Hendrix+Experience/_/Foxy+Lady" class="bbcode_track">Foxy Lady</a>, <a title="The Jimi Hendrix Experience &ndash; Hey Joe" href="http://www.last.fm/music/The+Jimi+Hendrix+Experience/_/Hey+Joe" class="bbcode_track">Hey Joe</a>, <a title="The Jimi Hendrix Experience &ndash; Voodoo Child (Slight Return)" href="http://www.last.fm/music/The+Jimi+Hendrix+Experience/_/Voodoo+Child+(Slight+Return)" class="bbcode_track">Voodoo Child (Slight Return)</a> and <a title="The Jimi Hendrix Experience &ndash; All Along the Watchtower" href="http://www.last.fm/music/The+Jimi+Hendrix+Experience/_/All+Along+the+Watchtower" class="bbcode_track">All Along the Watchtower</a>. Rounding out the Experience were <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Noel+Redding" class="bbcode_artist">Noel Redding</a> (1945–2003) and <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Mitch+Mitchell" class="bbcode_artist">Mitch Mitchell</a> (1947–2008) on bass and drums respectively.  Hendrix arrived in England in October 1966, and auditions were launched to find him a backing band.

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/The+Jimi+Hendrix+Experience">Read more about The Jimi Hendrix Experience on Last.fm</a>.

 START_ARTIST Washed Out ::: Perry, Georgia, USA ::: 
                Washed Out is Ernest Greene, a young guy from Perry, Georgia, USA who makes bedroom synthpop that sounds blurred and woozily evocative.  There’s a sense of longing and distance in Greene’s somber, filtered vocals, but it’s what he does compositionally that makes Washed Out stand out.  START_ARTIST Tiësto ::: Breda, the Netherlands ::: 
                Tijs Verwest, known as DJ Tiësto, was born in Breda, the Netherlands. He started DJing professionally at school and house parties in the early 1980s, and then moved on to become a resident DJ between 1985 and 1993 at several clubs in The Netherlands. It was at a club called 'The Spock' where things really picked up for Tiësto. He stopped producing hardcore/gabber tracks and started to produce his own sound from 10pm until 4am on weekends. In the mid 1990s, Tiësto started to produce <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/trance" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">trance</a> . He has since abandoned trance to play house.

 START_ARTIST Elliott Smith ::: Portland, Oregon ::: 
                Steven Paul &quot;Elliott&quot; Smith (August 6, 1969 – October 21, 2003) was an American songwriter and musician. Smith was born in Omaha, Nebraska, raised primarily in Texas, and resided for a significant portion of his life in Portland, Oregon, where he first gained popularity. His primary instrument was the guitar, but he was also proficient at piano, clarinet, bass, drums and harmonica. Smith had a distinctive vocal style characterized by his &quot;whispery, spiderweb-thin delivery&quot; and use of multi-tracking to create vocal harmonies.

 START_ARTIST Mogwai ::: Glasgow :::

They compose lengthy, mostly instrumental guitar-based pieces in the style of <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/post-rock" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">post-rock</a>, usually focused around the elaboration of a single theme, and are known traditionally for their quiet/loud dynamic, defined bass riffs, and an eminent ambient sound, sometimes dark and sometimes grand. The band first came to public attention after their performing the song &quot;Soul Sacrifice&quot; at the Woodstock Festival in 1969, when their Latin rock provided a contrast to other acts on the bill.  START_ARTIST Leonard Cohen ::: Montréal, Quebec, Canada :::

Musically, Cohen's early songs are based in folk music, in terms of both melody and instrumentation; from the 1970s, though, his work begins to show the influence of various types of popular and cabaret music.

 START_ARTIST Cream ::: London, England ::: 
                Cream was a 1960s three-piece British band consisting of bassist/lead vocalist <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Jack+Bruce" class="bbcode_artist">Jack Bruce</a>, guitarist/vocalist <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Eric+Clapton" class="bbcode_artist">Eric Clapton</a>, and drummer <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Ginger+Baker" class="bbcode_artist">Ginger Baker</a>, having formed in London, England. They were known as one of the first great power trios and supergroups of rock. Their sound was characterised by a hybrid of <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/blues" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">blues</a>, <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/hard%20rock" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">hard rock</a> and <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/psychedelic%20rock" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">psychedelic rock</a>. Cream combined Clapton's blues guitar playing with the powerful and airy voice and intense bass lines of Jack Bruce and the manic drumming of Ginger Baker.

 START_ARTIST Jefferson Airplane ::: San Francisco ::: 
                Jefferson Airplane was a <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/psychedelic%20rock" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">psychedelic rock</a> group formed in San Francisco. It was the first of several Bay Area psychedelic groups of the 1960s to become internationally known. The band was founded by singer <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Marty+Balin" class="bbcode_artist">Marty Balin</a> and guitarist <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Paul+Kantner" class="bbcode_artist">Paul Kantner</a> in 1965. With the addition of <span title="Unknown artist" class="bbcode_unknown">Signe Anderson</span>, their male-female singing style showed their folk music roots plus Balin's love of R&amp;B singing styles. In fact their dual lead vocals were a hallmark of their sound throughout the Airplane's career, as confirmed (to international acclaim) after <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Grace+Slick" class="bbcode_artist">Grace Slick</a> replaced Signe Anderson as the female singer.

 START_ARTIST Louis Armstrong ::: New Orleans ::: 
                Louis Armstrong (1901-1971) was a trumpet player, singer, and bandleader, and is widely regarded as one of the most influential artists in the history of jazz.  Armstrong was born and brought up in New Orleans, a culturally diverse town with a unique musical mix of creole, ragtime, marching bands, and blues. Although from an early age he was able to play music professionally, he didn't travel far from New Orleans until 1922, when he went to Chicago to join his mentor, <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/King+Oliver" class="bbcode_artist">King Oliver</a>.

 START_ARTIST Tears for Fears ::: Bath, England :::

Founder members <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Roland+Orzabal" class="bbcode_artist">Roland Orzabal</a> and <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Curt+Smith" class="bbcode_artist">Curt Smith</a> had been friends since their early teens and had already been in the shortlived <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/ska" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">ska</a> band <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Graduate" class="bbcode_artist">Graduate</a>. Initially associated with the <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/new%20wave" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">new wave</a> and <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/synthesiser" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">synthesiser</a> bands of the early 1980s, Tears For Fears' earlier work, as evidenced on their 1983 debut album <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Tears+for+Fears/The+Hurting">The Hurting</a> , was explicitly based around the emotional angst of adolescence.

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Tears+for+Fears">Read more about Tears for Fears on Last.fm</a>.
    
     END_ARTIST
 START_ARTIST Porcupine Tree ::: Hemel Hempstead, Hertfordshire, United Kingdom ::: 
                Porcupine Tree is a British rock band formed in Hemel Hempstead, Hertfordshire, United Kingdom in 1987. During the course of the band's history, it has at times incorporated psychedelic rock, alternative, ambient, electronic, and, most recently, metal and post-rock into its unique style of progressive rock.  Porcupine Tree started out as a &quot;fake&quot; band, the only real member being multi-instrumentalist <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Steven+Wilson" class="bbcode_artist">Steven Wilson</a>.

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Porcupine+Tree">Read more about Porcupine Tree on Last.fm</a>.
    
     END_ARTIST
 START_ARTIST Ne-Yo ::: Camden, Arkansas ::: 
                Shaffer Chimere Smith (born on October 18, 1979 in Camden, Arkansas), better known by his stage name Ne-Yo, is a Grammy Award winning American R&amp;B singer, producer and actor currently signed to Def Jam Records. In 2006 he released his debut album In My Own Words, which featured the hit single So Sick. The song reached #1 on the Billboard Hot 100 and helped his album debut at #1 on the Billboard 200.

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Ne-Yo">Read more about Ne-Yo on Last.fm</a>.

 START_ARTIST Scissor Sisters ::: New York City, NY, USA :::

The band was formed in 2000, by <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Jason+Sellards" class="bbcode_artist">Jason Sellards</a> (aka <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Jake+Shears" class="bbcode_artist">Jake Shears</a> - lead vocals) &amp; <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Scott+Hoffman" class="bbcode_artist">Scott Hoffman</a> (aka <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Babydaddy" class="bbcode_artist">Babydaddy</a> - keyboard / bass).  <span title="Unknown artist" class="bbcode_unknown">Randy Schrager</span> (aka <span title="Unknown artist" class="bbcode_unknown">Randy Real</span>), is the band's live drummer. <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Patrick+Seacor" class="bbcode_artist">Patrick Seacor</a> (aka <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Paddy+Boom" class="bbcode_artist">Paddy Boom</a>), left band in 2008. Lyrics are largely written by Shears / Babydaddy &amp; known for a mixture of wit &amp; tragedy.

 START_ARTIST Tricky ::: Knowle West, Bristol, England ::: 
                Adrian Thaws (born 27 January 1968), better known as Tricky, is a rapper and musician from Knowle West, Bristol, England who is important in the <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/trip-hop" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">trip-hop</a> scene (despite loathing the tag) and remains influential on the <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/british" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">british</a> scene more generally.  He is noted for an asthmatic whispering lyrical style that is half-rapped, half-sung. As a producer and a musician he is known for having an aversion to perfection preferring to build up a dark, rich and layered sound. Culturally, Tricky bridges white and black Britain particularly in his fusion of <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/rock" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">rock</a> and <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/hip-hop" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">hip-hop</a>, high art and pop culture.

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Tricky">Read more about Tricky on Last.fm</a>.

 START_ARTIST The Glitch Mob ::: Los Angeles, California ::: 
                The Glitch Mob is a three-piece electronic group from Los Angeles, California, composed of Ed Ma (<a href="http://www.last.fm/music/edIT" class="bbcode_artist">edIT</a>), Justin Boreta (<a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Boreta" class="bbcode_artist">Boreta</a>) and Josh Mayer (<a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Ooah" class="bbcode_artist">Ooah</a>). The group, originally a four-piece including <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Kraddy" class="bbcode_artist">Kraddy</a>, was formed in 2006 within the burgeoning Los Angeles bass-driven 'beat' scene. The Glitch Mob made a name for themselves playing live, choosing to perform with laptops and MIDI controllers. They have won fans through showcasing their chosen technology during performance solos gaining attention in Los Angeles and San Francisco...

 START_ARTIST Broken Bells ::: Los Angeles ::: 
                Broken Bells is an American <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/indie%20rock" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">indie rock</a> duo which formed in 2009 in Los Angeles. The band consists of <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/James+Mercer" class="bbcode_artist">James Mercer</a> (vocals, guitar) and Brian &quot;<a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Danger+Mouse" class="bbcode_artist">Danger Mouse</a>&quot; Burton (multiple instruments, production). Mercer is a member of the indie rock band <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/The+Shins" class="bbcode_artist">The Shins</a> and Burton is a member of <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Gnarls+Barkley" class="bbcode_artist">Gnarls Barkley</a> and <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/DANGERDOOM" class="bbcode_artist">DANGERDOOM</a>, as well as being a respected producer for such artists as <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Beck" class="bbcode_artist">Beck</a>, <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Gorillaz" class="bbcode_artist">Gorillaz</a>, <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/The+Rapture" class="bbcode_artist">The Rapture</a> and <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/The+Black+Keys" class="bbcode_artist">The Black Keys</a>.  The debut self-titled album by Broken Bells was released on Columbia Records on March 9, 2010. The first single from the record, &quot;The High Road&quot;, was released on December 21, 2009.

 START_ARTIST A Tribe Called Quest ::: Queens, New York City ::: 
                A Tribe Called Quest was an influential hip hop group of the 1990s, originally formed in Queens, New York City in 1985. The group is composed of <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Q-Tip" class="bbcode_artist">Q-Tip</a>, <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Phife+Dawg" class="bbcode_artist">Phife Dawg</a>, and DJ <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Ali+Shaheed+Muhammad" class="bbcode_artist">Ali Shaheed Muhammad</a>. A fourth member, <span title="Unknown artist" class="bbcode_unknown">Jarobi White</span>, was an intermittent collaborator appearing on their first album, but he left the group soon after, although he is mentioned as a 'sometimes' member on their third album liner notes. Along with <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/De+La+Soul" class="bbcode_artist">De La Soul</a>, the group was a central part of the <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Native+Tongues+Posse" class="bbcode_artist">Native Tongues Posse</a>, and enjoyed the most commercial success out of all the groups to emerge from that collective.

 START_ARTIST a-ha ::: Oslo, Norway ::: 
                a-ha was a Norwegian band that was globally successful from the 1980s until their split in 2010. The trio, composed of lead vocalist <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Morten+Harket" class="bbcode_artist">Morten Harket</a>, guitarist <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Paul+Waaktaar-Savoy" class="bbcode_artist">Paul Waaktaar-Savoy</a> and keyboardist <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Magne+Furuholmen" class="bbcode_artist">Magne Furuholmen</a>, formed in 1982 and left Oslo, Norway for London in order to make a career in the music business.   The origin of the name a-ha comes from the lyric of an early song. After checking dictionaries in several languages, they found out that 'a-ha' was an international way of expressing recognition, with positive connotations. It was short, a-ha was easy to say and somewhat unusual. 

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/a-ha">Read more about a-ha on Last.fm</a>.

 START_ARTIST John Lennon ::: Liverpool, UK ::: 
                John Winston Ono Lennon (9 October 1940 – 8 December 1980) was an English musician, singer, <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/songwriter" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">songwriter</a>, and peace activist, born in Liverpool, UK who gained worldwide fame as a founding member of <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/The+Beatles" class="bbcode_artist">The Beatles</a>. With <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Paul+McCartney" class="bbcode_artist">Paul McCartney</a>, Lennon formed one of the most influential and successful songwriting partnerships of the 20th century and &quot;wrote some of the most popular music in <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/rock%20and%20roll" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">rock and roll</a> history&quot;. He is ranked the second most successful songwriter in UK singles chart history after <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Paul+McCartney" class="bbcode_artist">Paul McCartney</a>.   

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/John+Lennon">Read more about John Lennon on Last.fm</a>.

 START_ARTIST Lou Reed ::: Brooklyn, New York, USA ::: 
                Lou Reed (born March 2, 1942) is an American <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/rock" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">rock</a> artist originally from Brooklyn, New York, USA. Especially while a member of the <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/The+Velvet+Underground" class="bbcode_artist">The Velvet Underground</a> in the 1960s, Reed broke new ground for the <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/rock" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">rock</a> genre in several important dimensions, introducing more mature and intellectual themes to what was then considered a largely simplistic genre of music.  In 1964 Reed moved to New York City and began working as an in-house songwriter for Pickwick Records.

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Lou+Reed">Read more about Lou Reed on Last.fm</a>.

Thievery Corporation is on the <a href="http://www.last.fm/label/Eighteenth+Street+Lounge" class="bbcode_label">Eighteenth Street Lounge</a> record label named after the DC club owned by Eric Hilton, but several of their singles and EP's appear on the <a href="http://www.last.fm/label/4AD" class="bbcode_label">4AD</a> and <a href="http://www.last.fm/label/!K7" class="bbcode_label">!K7</a> labels.

 START_ARTIST Enter Shikari ::: St Albans, Hertfordshire, England :::

The incorporation of electronic genres has become more prominent in their music throughout the band's history. Lyrically, their music tackles political, social and scientific issues.

 START_ARTIST Matchbox Twenty ::: Orlando :::

 START_ARTIST The Stone Roses ::: Manchester ::: 
                The Stone Roses are an influential alternative rock band which formed in Manchester, England in 1984. For most of their career, the band consisted of Ian Brown (vocals), John Squire (guitar), Gary &quot;Mani&quot; Mounfield (bass) and Alan &quot;Reni&quot; Wren (drums).   Meshing '60s-styled guitar pop with an understated '80s dance beat, the band defined the British guitar pop scene of the late '80s and early '90s.  START_ARTIST Ludwig van Beethoven ::: Bonn, Germany ::: 
                Ludwig van Beethoven (16 December 1770 – 26 March 1827) was a composer of the transitional period between the late Classical and early Romantic eras. He was born in Bonn, Germany.  Beethoven is widely regarded as one of the greatest masters of musical construction, sometimes sketching the architecture of a movement before he had decided upon the subject matter. He was one of the first composers to systematically and consistently use interlocking thematic devices, or “germ-motives”, to achieve unity between movements in long compositions.

 START_ARTIST Ennio Morricone ::: Rome ::: 
                Ennio Morricone (born 10 November 1928 in Rome) is an Italian composer especially noted for his film scores. He has composed the scores of more than 500 motion pictures and television series, in a career lasting over 50 years. His scores have been included in over 30 award-winning films as well as several symphonic and choral pieces. Morricone is most famous for his work in the Spaghetti Westerns directed by his friend Sergio Leone.

 START_ARTIST Ludovico Einaudi ::: Italy ::: 
                Ludovico Einaudi (born 23 November 1955 in Turin) is a modern-day Italian composer and pianist particularly noted for the use of developing melodious phrases in his piano compositions.  He began his musical training at the Conservatorio Verdi in Milan, Italy, gaining a diploma in composition. Later, he studied with <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Luciano+Berio" class="bbcode_artist">Luciano Berio</a>. In 1982, he gained a scholarship to the Tanglewood Music Festival. He currently resides on a vineyard in the Italian region of Piemonte.  Although Einaudi would prefer not to be labeled as any particular type of composer, he is generally considered a Minimalist. 

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Ludovico+Einaudi">Read more about Ludovico Einaudi on Last.fm</a>.

The roots of Lamb of God were planted in the year 1990, when Mark Morton, Chris Adler and John Campbell were friends at Virginia Commonwealth University. Centered on guitarist, songwriter, and producer <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Tom+Scholz" class="bbcode_artist">Tom Scholz</a>, a former product designer at Polaroid Corporation and an MIT engineering student, the band's best known works include the singles &quot;<a title="Boston &ndash; More Than a Feeling" href="http://www.last.fm/music/Boston/_/More+Than+a+Feeling" class="bbcode_track">More Than a Feeling</a>&quot;, &quot;<a title="Boston &ndash; Peace Of Mind" href="http://www.last.fm/music/Boston/_/Peace+Of+Mind" class="bbcode_track">Peace Of Mind</a>&quot;, &quot;<a title="Boston &ndash; Foreplay/Long Time" href="http://www.last.fm/music/Boston/_/Foreplay%2FLong+Time" class="bbcode_track">Foreplay/Long Time</a>&quot;, &quot;<a title="Boston &ndash; Don't Look Back" href="http://www.last.fm/music/Boston/_/Don%27t+Look+Back" class="bbcode_track">Don't Look Back</a>&quot;, and &quot;<a title="Boston &ndash; Amanda" href="http://www.last.fm/music/Boston/_/Amanda" class="bbcode_track">Amanda</a>&quot;. Their 1976 self-titled debut is the second biggest-selling debut album of all-time in the U.S.

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Boston">Read more about Boston on Last.fm</a>.
    
     END_ARTIST
 START_ARTIST Yo La Tengo ::: Hoboken, New Jersey ::: 
                Yo La Tengo is an <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/american">American</a> <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/indie%20rock" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">indie rock</a> band formed in Hoboken, New Jersey in 1984. Since 1992, the lineup has consisted of <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ira_Kaplan" rel="nofollow">Ira Kaplan</a> (guitars, vocals), <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Georgia_Hubley" rel="nofollow">Georgia Hubley</a> (drums, vocals), and <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/James_McNew" rel="nofollow">James McNew</a> (bass, vocals).  Despite achieving limited <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/mainstream" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">mainstream</a> success, Yo La Tengo has been called &quot;the quintessential critics' band&quot; and maintain a strong cult following. Additionally, the band is renowned for its encyclopedic repertoire of <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/cover" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">cover</a> songs both in <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/live" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">live</a> performance and on record.  Formation and Early History: <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/1984" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">1984</a>–<a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/1985" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">1985</a> 

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Yo+La+Tengo">Read more about Yo La Tengo on Last.fm</a>.

 START_ARTIST Enya ::: Gweedore, County Donegal, Ireland ::: 
                Eithne Patricia Ní Bhraonáin (born May 17, 1961 in Gweedore, County Donegal, Ireland), known simply as Enya, is a Grammy award winning and Academy award nominated Irish singer, instrumentalist and composer. She began her musical career in 1980, when she briefly joined her family band <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Clannad" class="bbcode_artist">Clannad</a>, before leaving to pursue her solo career. Her album Watermark, which was released in 1988, propelled her to international recognition and she became known for her unique sound, which is characterized by voice-layering, folk melodies, synthesized backdrops and ethereal reverberations.

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Enya">Read more about Enya on Last.fm</a>.
    
     END_ARTIST
 START_ARTIST Imogen Heap ::: Havering, Outer London ::: 
                Imogen Heap (born December 9, 1977, in Havering, Outer London) is a British <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/singer-songwriter" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">singer-songwriter</a> / <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/electronica" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">electronica</a> artist. She is known for her work as part of the musical duo <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Frou+Frou" class="bbcode_artist">Frou Frou</a> from 2002-3, and for her solo albums, which she writes, produces, and mixes. She has released a series of solo albums including Ellipse (in 2009), a North American chart success that earned Heap two Grammy nominations and won her the Best Engineered Album (Non-Classical) award.  

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Imogen+Heap">Read more about Imogen Heap on Last.fm</a>.

 START_ARTIST Ella Fitzgerald ::: Newport News, VA ::: 
                Ella Jane Fitzgerald (April 25, 1917 in Newport News, VA – June 15, 1996), also known as Lady Ella (the First Lady of Song), was one of the most influential jazz singers of the 20th Century, the winner of thirteen Grammy Awards, the National Medal of Art presented by President Ronald Reagan and the Presidential Medal of Freedom presented by President George H. W. Bush.   Gifted with a three-octave vocal range, she was noted for her purity of tone, near faultless phrasing and intonation, and a &quot;horn-like&quot; improvisational ability, particularly in her scat singing.   

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Ella+Fitzgerald">Read more about Ella Fitzgerald on Last.fm</a>.
    
     END_ARTIST

The original members were <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Stephan+Jenkins" class="bbcode_artist">Stephan Jenkins</a> (singer, songwriter, electric guitar), <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Kevin+Cadogan" class="bbcode_artist">Kevin Cadogan</a> (guitar), <span title="Unknown artist" class="bbcode_unknown">Adrian Burley</span> (drums), and <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Jason+Slater" class="bbcode_artist">Jason Slater</a> (bass guitar). The band's original line-up changed several times before the release of the group's debut album, and again shortly after the release of the band's second album <a title="Third Eye Blind - Blue" href="http://www.last.fm/music/Third+Eye+Blind/Blue" class="bbcode_album">Blue</a> — at which point the band's main guitarist <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Kevin+Cadogan" class="bbcode_artist">Kevin Cadogan</a> was released from the band under circumstances that still elicit controversy among fans.

 START_ARTIST The Gaslight Anthem ::: New Brunswick, New Jersey :::

Since forming in 2006, they have released four full-length albums and an EP. They were described by Kerrang! magazine as “the best new band you’ll hear in 2008.” The lineup consists of <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Brian+Fallon" class="bbcode_artist">Brian Fallon</a> (vocals and guitar), Alex Levine (bass), Benny Horowitz (drums), and Alex Rosamilia (guitar).  The Gaslight Anthem’s music embraces many elements of blues, classic rock, and punk rock. The band has described their sound as “Bruce Springsteen singing for a Cure cover band, with a tinge more aggression.

 START_ARTIST Creed ::: Tallahassee, Florida ::: 
                Creed is an American <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/post-grunge" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">post-grunge</a> band, from Tallahassee, Florida, that became commercially successful during the late 90's.  Creed formed in 1994 with their debut album, <a title="Creed - My Own Prison" href="http://www.last.fm/music/Creed/My+Own+Prison" class="bbcode_album">My Own Prison</a>. After hearing them play live, Diana Meltzer of Wind-Up Records decided to sign the band to her label. After making it more radio friendly, the album was re-released by Wind-Up across the country and became a success, reaching the Top 40 of the Billboard 200. My Own Prison is, as of now, 6-times platinum.  

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Creed">Read more about Creed on Last.fm</a>.

 START_ARTIST Rod Stewart ::: London, England ::: 
                Roderick David &quot;Rod&quot; Stewart, CBE (born 10 January 1945)  is a British singer-songwriter born and raised in London, England and currently residing in Epping. He is of Scottish and English lineage.  With his distinctive raspy singing voice, <a href="http://www.rodstewart.com" rel="nofollow">Rod Stewart</a>  came to prominence in the late 1960s and early 1970s with <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/+noredirect/The+Jeff+Beck+Group" class="bbcode_artist">The Jeff Beck Group</a> (1967-1969) and then <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Faces" class="bbcode_artist">Faces</a>. He launched his solo career in 1969 with his début album An Old Raincoat Won't Ever Let You Down (US: The Rod Stewart Album).

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Rod+Stewart">Read more about Rod Stewart on Last.fm</a>.

 START_ARTIST Ludacris ::: Champaign, Illinois ::: 
                Christopher Brian Bridges (born September 11, 1977 in Champaign, Illinois), better known by his stage name Ludacris, is a Grammy award winning American rapper, SAG award winning actor and co-founder of the label Disturbing Tha Peace. He is the highest selling Southern hip hop solo artist of all time with over 15 million units sold in the United States and around 20 million records sold worldwide. He released his debut album Incognegro in 1999 and has since released a further seven albums. His ninth studio album, Ludaversal, will be released sometime in 2012. 

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Ludacris">Read more about Ludacris on Last.fm</a>.

 START_ARTIST Serj Tankian ::: Los Angeles :::

He started as a singer in the <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/alternative%20metal" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">alternative metal</a> band <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/System+of+a+Down" class="bbcode_artist">System of a Down</a> and after they went on hiatus he continued his career as a solo artist and producer. He is known for his gritty yet wide vocal range. His solo output mixes various styles and genres, including metal, rock and Armenian musical motifs.  At age five, Serj Tankian moved with his parents to Los Angeles, California.

Mötley Crüe has sold more than 80 million album copies worldwide, including 25 million in the U.S.  The band members have often been noted for their hard-living lifestyles; all members have had numerous brushes with the law, have spent time in jail, have suffered long addictions to alcohol and drugs...

 START_ARTIST Sepultura ::: Belo Horizonte, Brazil ::: 
                Sepultura is a Brazilian metal band that formed in 1983 in Belo Horizonte, Brazil. The band was a major force in the <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/death%20metal" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">death metal</a>, <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/thrash%20metal" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">thrash metal</a> and ultimately <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/groove%20metal" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">groove metal</a> realms during the late 1980s and early 1990s.  Their name means &quot;grave&quot; in Portuguese, which they chose after Max Cavalera, one of the founding members, was translating the lyrics of the <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Mot%C3%B6rhead" class="bbcode_artist">Mot&ouml;rhead</a> song &quot;Dancing on Your Grave&quot;.  Sepultura was formed by <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Max+Cavalera" class="bbcode_artist">Max Cavalera</a>  (guitars and vocals), his younger brother <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Igor+Cavalera" class="bbcode_artist">Igor Cavalera</a> (drums), <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Paulo+Pinto" class="bbcode_artist">Paulo Pinto</a> (bass) and Jairo Guedes (guitars).

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Sepultura">Read more about Sepultura on Last.fm</a>.

 START_ARTIST Plain White T's ::: Illinois, United States :::

They are best known for &quot;Hey There Delilah&quot;, an acoustic song performed solely by singer Tom Higgenson originally released in 2005 and later hit #1 in the US in 2007.  For over a decade, Plain White T's have been playing to packed audiences craving for that perfect pop-punk punch. Their journey, which began in a small suburban basement playing covers, has taken the band to Warped Tour three times, and landed them opening slots for bands like Jimmy Eat World and AFI.

The band was founded by lead singer Courtney Taylor-Taylor, keyboardist Zia McCabe, guitarist Peter Holmström, and drummer Eric Hedford. Hedford left in 1998 to be replaced by Taylor-Taylor's cousin <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Brent+Deboer" class="bbcode_artist">Brent Deboer</a>. The band's name is a pun on the name of American pop artist Andy Warhol.  The Dandy Warhols are strongly influenced by The Brian Jonestown Massacre, The Velvet Underground, The Beach Boys, Simon and Garfunkel, The Beatles, The Shadows and The Rolling Stones.

 START_ARTIST Billie Holiday ::: Philadelphia ::: 
                Billie Holiday (Eleanora Fagan Gough, Philadelphia, PA, April 7, 1915 – New York City, NY, July 17, 1959) was an American jazz singer and songwriter.  Nicknamed Lady Day by her loyal friend and musical partner <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Lester+Young" class="bbcode_artist">Lester Young</a>, Holiday was a germinal influence on jazz and pop singing. Her vocal style, strongly inspired by jazz instrumentalists, pioneered a new way of manipulating phrasing and tempo. Above all, she was admired for her deeply personal and intimate approach to singing. Critic John Bush wrote that she &quot;changed the art of American pop vocals forever.

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Billie+Holiday">Read more about Billie Holiday on Last.fm</a>.

 START_ARTIST KT Tunstall ::: St Andrews, Scotland ::: 
                Kate Victoria Tunstall, better known as KT Tunstall (born 23 June 1975 in St Andrews, Scotland), is a Scottish singer-songwriter and guitarist. She broke into the public eye with a live solo performance of her song &quot;Black Horse and the Cherry Tree&quot; on Later... with Jools Holland. She has enjoyed commercial and critical success since, picking up three nominations before winning a BRIT Award, and a Grammy Award nomination. She is also the recipient of an Ivor Novello Award.  

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/KT+Tunstall">Read more about KT Tunstall on Last.fm</a>.
    
     END_ARTIST
 START_ARTIST The Animals ::: Newcastle ::: 
                The Animals were a British <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/rock" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">rock</a> band of the 1960s, formed in Newcastle. They were part of the <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/british%20invasion" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">british invasion</a>, being one of the most popular bands of their era. Known for their gritty, raw, bluesy sound and hard-voiced frontman <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Eric+Burdon" class="bbcode_artist">Eric Burdon</a>, as exemplified by their signature songs <a title="The Animals &ndash; House of the Rising Sun" href="http://www.last.fm/music/+noredirect/The+Animals/_/House+of+the+Rising+Sun" class="bbcode_track">House of the Rising Sun</a> and <a title="The Animals &ndash; Don't Let Me Be Misunderstood" href="http://www.last.fm/music/The+Animals/_/Don%27t+Let+Me+Be+Misunderstood" class="bbcode_track">Don't Let Me Be Misunderstood</a>, the band underwent numerous personnel changes, while influencing the later <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/heavy%20metal" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">heavy metal</a> music with the riffs of their rock songs such as <a title="The Animals &ndash; We Gotta Get Out Of This Place" href="http://www.last.fm/music/+noredirect/The+Animals/_/We+Gotta+Get+Out+Of+This+Place" class="bbcode_track">We Gotta Get Out Of This Place</a> and <a title="The Animals &ndash; It's My Life" href="http://www.last.fm/music/The+Animals/_/It%27s+My+Life" class="bbcode_track">It's My Life</a>.

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/The+Animals">Read more about The Animals on Last.fm</a>.
    
     END_ARTIST
 START_ARTIST Al Green ::: Forrest City, Arkansas ::: 
                Reverend Albert Green (born April 13 1946 in Forrest City, Arkansas) is an American Grammy award winning <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/soul" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">soul</a> and <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/gospel" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">gospel</a> singer who enjoyed great popularity in the <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/70s" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">70s</a> with the hit singles <a title="Al Green &ndash; Let's Stay Together" href="http://www.last.fm/music/Al+Green/_/Let%27s+Stay+Together" class="bbcode_track">Let's Stay Together</a>, <a title="Al Green &ndash; Tired Of Being Alone" href="http://www.last.fm/music/Al+Green/_/Tired+Of+Being+Alone" class="bbcode_track">Tired Of Being Alone</a> and <a title="Al Green &ndash; You Oughta Be With Me" href="http://www.last.fm/music/+noredirect/Al+Green/_/You+Oughta+Be+With+Me" class="bbcode_track">You Oughta Be With Me</a>. Green boasted a voice capable of both fluid high streams of sugar and deep south growls and rasps. He has sold over 20 million records worldwide and was inducted into The Rock and Roll Hall of Fame in 1995, being referred to as &quot;one of the most gifted purveyors of soul music.&quot; 

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Al+Green">Read more about Al Green on Last.fm</a>.
    
     END_ARTIST
 START_ARTIST August Burns Red ::: Manheim, Pennsylvania ::: 
                August Burns Red is a band from Manheim, Pennsylvania. Formed in 2003, the group began their first performances while a majority of the members were attending their senior year of high school, and soon began playing shows around Lancaster, before being signed to <a href="http://www.last.fm/label/CI+Records" class="bbcode_label">CI Records</a>, and afterward, <a href="http://www.last.fm/label/solid+state+records" class="bbcode_label">solid state records</a>. The group is primarily known for their heavy breakdowns, highly melodic guitar riffs and odd-meter riffs. They state <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Between+the+Buried+and+Me" class="bbcode_artist">Between the Buried and Me</a>, <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Misery+Signals" class="bbcode_artist">Misery Signals</a> and <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Hopesfall" class="bbcode_artist">Hopesfall</a> as their main influences. 

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/August+Burns+Red">Read more about August Burns Red on Last.fm</a>.
    
     END_ARTIST
 START_ARTIST Netsky ::: Edegem ::: 
                Rarely have we seen someone rise through the ranks as quickly as 24 year old Boris Daenen, a.k.a Netsky. Having a Belgian passport doesn’t often turn D+B heads, so you can be sure it’s his tunes which do the talking! Having secured releases on some of the biggest labels in the scene, gained DJ support from the likes of Friction, Hype, Fabio and London Elektricity, the young Belgian from Edegem near Antwerp earned a nomination as “Best Upcoming Producer” at the Drum + Bass Arena Awards in 2008 and fulfilled this ambition two years on with is “Best Newcomer Producer” award in 2010. 

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Netsky">Read more about Netsky on Last.fm</a>.

 START_ARTIST Tracy Chapman ::: Cleveland, Ohio,U.S. ::: 
                Tracy Chapman (born March 30, 1964) is an <a href="http://www.last.fm/place/united%20states">American</a> <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/singer-songwriter" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">singer-songwriter</a>, best known for the singles &quot;Fast Car&quot;, &quot;Talkin' Bout a Revolution&quot;, &quot;Baby Can I Hold You&quot;, and &quot;Give Me One Reason.&quot; She is a multi-platinum and multi-Grammy award-winning artist.  Born in <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/cleveland">Cleveland</a>, <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/ohio">Ohio</a>,U.S., Tracy Chapman began playing guitar and writing songs as a child. She received a scholarship through <a href="http://www.abetterchance.org/" rel="nofollow">A Better Chance</a> that allowed her to attend Wooster School in Connecticut, and was eventually accepted to Tufts University in Medford, Massachusetts.

Kelly</a>.  START_ARTIST Céline Dion ::: Charlemagne, Quebec, Canada ::: 
                Céline Marie Claudette Dion (born March 30, 1968 in Charlemagne, Quebec, Canada) is a Canadian singer. Born to a large impoverished family, Dion emerged as a teen star in the French-speaking world after her manager and future husband René Angélil mortgaged his home to finance her first record.  In 1990, she released the anglophone album Unison, establishing herself as a viable pop artist in North America and other English-speaking areas of the world.  

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/C%C3%A9line+Dion">Read more about Céline Dion on Last.fm</a>.

 START_ARTIST My Morning Jacket ::: Louisville, Kentucky, United States ::: 
                My Morning Jacket is a rock band which formed in 1998 in Louisville, Kentucky, United States. The band consists of Jim James (vocals, guitar), Carl Broemel (guitar), &quot;Two Tone&quot; Tommy Blankenship (bass), Bo Koster (keyboards) and Patrick Hallahan (drums). The band is best known for their reverb-soaked sound and their enthusiastic live shows. My Morning Jacket is signed with ATO Records. The band's style is a blend of alternative, alt country, folk rock and psychedelic rock.

 START_ARTIST Sleeping with Sirens ::: Orlando, Florida :::

The first album debuted at number 7 on Billboard's Top Heatseekers chart, and at number 36 on Top Independent Albums. Their second album was released on May 10, 2011.  START_ARTIST Machine Head ::: Oakland, California ::: 
                Machine Head is an American metal band, formed in 1992 in Oakland, California. Founded by former <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Vio-Lence" class="bbcode_artist">Vio-Lence</a> guitarist Robert Flynn and Adam Duce, and has only had 3 personnel changes since its inception. The current lineup of the band comprises of Robb Flynn (vocals, guitar), Adam Duce (bass), Phil Demmel (guitar), and Dave McClain (drums). Machine Head is one of the pioneering bands in the New Wave of American Heavy Metal.
