 START_ARTIST Gogol Bordello ::: New York ::: 
                Combining elements of <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/punk" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">punk</a>, <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/gypsy" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">gypsy</a> music, and Brechtian <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/cabaret" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">cabaret</a>, <a href="http://www.gogolbordello.com" rel="nofollow">Gogol Bordello</a>  tells the story of New York's immigrant diaspora through debauchery, humor, and surreal costumes. Leader and singer <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Eugene+H%C3%BCtz" class="bbcode_artist">Eugene H&uuml;tz</a>'s taste in music was spun out of black-market tapes of the <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/The+Birthday+Party" class="bbcode_artist">The Birthday Party</a> and <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Einst%C3%BCrzende+Neubauten" class="bbcode_artist">Einst&uuml;rzende Neubauten</a> in his native Ukraine.  After being evacuated to Western Ukraine in 1986 following the Chernobyl disaster, Hütz became enamored of the mystical, outsider qualities of gypsy music.

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Gogol+Bordello">Read more about Gogol Bordello on Last.fm</a>.
    
     END_ARTIST
 START_ARTIST Digitalism ::: Hamburg, Germany ::: 
                Digitalism is an <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/electro%20house" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">electro house</a> duo founded in 2004 in Hamburg, Germany and consisting of <span title="Unknown artist" class="bbcode_unknown">Jens 'Jence' Moelle</span> and <span title="Unknown artist" class="bbcode_unknown">İsmail 'Isi' Tüfekçi</span>. They are signed to French label <a href="http://www.last.fm/label/Kitsun%C3%A9+Music" class="bbcode_label">Kitsun&eacute; Music</a>.  Digitalism has remixed tracks for The Presets, Tom Vek, The Futureheads, Daft Punk, Tiga, Klaxons, White Stripes, Monk, Depeche Mode, Cut Copy and many others, including a re-edit of &quot;Fire in Cairo&quot; by The Cure (entitled &quot;Digitalism in Cairo&quot;). Their tracks and remixes are played by DJs such as Erol Alkan, Soulwax, Boys Noize and Justice.

 START_ARTIST Manu Chao ::: Paris, France ::: 
                Manu Chao (born José-Manuel Thomas Arthur Chao on 21 June 1961 in Paris, France) is a singer of French and Spanish (Basque, Galician) origin.  Heavily influenced by the UK rock scene, particularly The Clash, The Jam and Dr. Feelgood, Chao and other musicians formed the Spanish/English rockabilly group <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Hot+Pants" class="bbcode_artist">Hot Pants</a> in the mid-1980s. The group released a demo entitled &quot;Mala Vida&quot; in 1984, which received plenty of local critical praise but otherwise gained them little attention.

 START_ARTIST Paolo Nutini ::: Paisley, Scotland ::: 
                Paolo Giovanni Nutini (b. 1987) is a Scottish  <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/singer-songwriter" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">singer-songwriter</a>.  His influences include <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/David+Bowie" class="bbcode_artist">David Bowie</a>, <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Damien+Rice" class="bbcode_artist">Damien Rice</a>, <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Oasis" class="bbcode_artist">Oasis</a>, <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/The+Beatles" class="bbcode_artist">The Beatles</a>, <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/U2" class="bbcode_artist">U2</a>, <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Pink+Floyd" class="bbcode_artist">Pink Floyd</a> and <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Fleetwood+Mac" class="bbcode_artist">Fleetwood Mac</a>.  Born on born 9th January 1987 in Paisley, Scotland, his father is of Italian descent and his mother Glaswegian, although his father's family have been in Scotland for four generations.  Nutini had no formal music training, and was expecting to follow his father into the family fish and chip shop business. He was first encouraged to sing by his music-loving grandfather and a teacher at his school who recognised his talent.

After Lynott died, various incarnations of the band have emerged over the years culminating in a more stable line-up based around guitarists <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Scott+Gorham" class="bbcode_artist">Scott Gorham</a> and <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/John+Sykes" class="bbcode_artist">John Sykes</a>. Over the band's 20 year career, it has released five studio albums, four EPs and ten top fifty singles in the UK.  The band is named after a line in the BBC TV mini-series The Singing Detective which says that the word &quot;elbow&quot; is the most sensuous word in the English language...

 START_ARTIST Frédéric Chopin ::: Żelazowa Wola, Poland ::: 
                Frédéric François Chopin (1810 –1849) is one of the most famous, influential, and admired composers and virtuoso pianists of the Romantic era.  He was born Fryderyk Franciszek Chopin, of Polish and French parentage, on 1st March 1810 in the village of Żelazowa Wola, Poland. In Warsaw he was hailed as a child prodigy and as the &quot;second Mozart&quot; for his piano and composition skill, for which the composer Robert Schumann complimented the talented pianist: &quot;Hats off, gentlemen, a genius!&quot; Due to the political situation in Poland, he left his country for France at the age of twenty.

They pioneered electronic music in the <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/70s" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">70s</a> and are considered one of the most important and influential bands of their genre, often described as &quot;the godfathers of electronic music&quot;.  START_ARTIST Puddle of Mudd ::: Kansas City ::: 
                Puddle of Mudd is an American <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/post-grunge" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">post-grunge</a> band. They achieved success on rock radio and some success in the mainstream, and their major-label debut Come Clean has sold over 5 million copies. To date the band has sold over 7 million albums, and have had a string of #1 mainstream rock singles in the United States.  START_ARTIST Mudvayne ::: Peoria, IL :::

The musical styles of their first two albums were highly innovative, combining elements of <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/progressive%20metal" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">progressive metal</a> with <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/alternative%20metal" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">alternative metal</a> and were considered to be a <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/math%20metal" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">math metal</a> band for this sound, although the band's later albums changed direction. The band is best recognizable by their strong drumming, complex bass playing, heavy, gruff and usually angered vocals, heavy guitars and riffs, complex time signatures and frequent rhythm changes. Mudvayne sold over 6,000,000 copies worldwide.

 START_ARTIST Brad Paisley ::: Glen Dale, West Virginia ::: 
                Brad Paisley (born October 28, 1972) is an American country music singer and songwriter from Glen Dale, West Virginia.  Brad Paisley has stated that his love of country music stems from his maternal grandfather, who gave Paisley his first guitar at age 8 and taught him how to play. At age 12, Paisley wrote his first song, and by 13 he was the opening act for country singers.  Paisley graduated from John Marshall High School in Glen Dale and enrolled at Belmont University (from 1993 to 1995). While in college, he met Frank Rogers, a fellow student who went on to serve as his producer.

The band split in early 2009, their last recording being a cover of the <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Gnarls+Barkley" class="bbcode_artist">Gnarls Barkley</a> song &quot;<a title="Violent Femmes &ndash; Crazy" href="http://www.last.fm/music/Violent+Femmes/_/Crazy" class="bbcode_track">Crazy</a>&quot;, a response to Gnarls Barkley's cover of the Femmes song &quot;<a title="Gnarls Barkley &ndash; Gone Daddy Gone" href="http://www.last.fm/music/Gnarls+Barkley/_/Gone+Daddy+Gone" class="bbcode_track">Gone Daddy Gone</a>&quot; released the previous year.

 START_ARTIST The Byrds ::: Los Angeles, California ::: 
                The Byrds were a popular American <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/rock" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">rock</a> band formed in Los Angeles, California in 1964. They are considered one of the most important and influential bands of the 19<a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/60s" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">60s</a>.   Their music bridged the gaps between the socially and spiritually conscious <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/folk" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">folk</a> music of <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Bob+Dylan" class="bbcode_artist">Bob Dylan</a>, and the studio trickery of <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/The+Beach+Boys" class="bbcode_artist">The Beach Boys</a>. Throughout their career they helped forge such subgenres as <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/folk%20rock" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">folk rock</a>, <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/raga%20rock" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">raga rock</a>, <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/psychedelic%20rock" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">psychedelic rock</a>, <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/jangle%20pop" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">jangle pop</a>, and – on their 1968 classic <a title="The Byrds - Sweetheart Of The Rodeo" href="http://www.last.fm/music/The+Byrds/Sweetheart+Of+The+Rodeo" class="bbcode_album">Sweetheart Of The Rodeo</a> – <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/country%20rock" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">country rock</a> inviting <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Gram+Parsons" class="bbcode_artist">Gram Parsons</a> on rhythm guitar.

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/The+Byrds">Read more about The Byrds on Last.fm</a>.

 START_ARTIST Patti Smith ::: Chicago, Illinois, USA ::: 
                Patricia Lee &quot;Patti&quot; Smith (born December 30, 1946) is an American singer, poet and visual artist who was a highly influential component of the New York <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/punk" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">punk</a> rock movement with her 1975 début album <a title="Patti Smith - Horses" href="http://www.last.fm/music/Patti+Smith/Horses" class="bbcode_album">Horses</a>. Called the &quot;Godmother of Punk&quot;, she integrated the beat <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/poetry" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">poetry</a> performance style with three-chord rock. Smith's most widely known song is <a title="Patti Smith &ndash; Because the Night" href="http://www.last.fm/music/Patti+Smith/_/Because+the+Night" class="bbcode_track">Because the Night</a>, which was co-written with <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Bruce+Springsteen" class="bbcode_artist">Bruce Springsteen</a> and reached number 13 on the Billboard Hot 100 chart in 1978. In 2007, she was inducted into the Rock and Roll Hall of Fame. 

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Patti+Smith">Read more about Patti Smith on Last.fm</a>.

 START_ARTIST Cocteau Twins ::: Grangemouth, Scotland, UK ::: 
                Cocteau Twins were an innovative and influential Scottish <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/dream%20pop" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">dream pop</a> band. Forming in 1979 in Grangemouth, Scotland, UK (the name taken from an obscure song by fellow Scots <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Simple+Minds" class="bbcode_artist">Simple Minds</a>), they built a sound based on woozy atmospherics and singer <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Elizabeth+Fraser" class="bbcode_artist">Elizabeth Fraser</a>'s unmatchable vocals, most of which featured lyrics of made-up words and words plucked at random from the dictionary.   Their first release was &quot;<a title="Cocteau Twins - Garlands" href="http://www.last.fm/music/Cocteau+Twins/Garlands" class="bbcode_album">Garlands</a>&quot; in 1982 on 4AD Records, which was received well. Founding member Will Heggie left the group in 1983 and soon joined fellow Grangemouth band <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Lowlife" class="bbcode_artist">Lowlife</a>.

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Cocteau+Twins">Read more about Cocteau Twins on Last.fm</a>.

The band name was taken from the famous children's author Shel Silverstein. In Christmas of 2001, he joined the band after Shane Told helped him learn the music for the songs. Following a rehearsal on Boxing Day (December 26) in 2001, he officially debuted with Silverstein.

 START_ARTIST Antonio Vivaldi ::: Venice ::: 
                Antonio Lucio Vivaldi (1678-1741) was a Venetian composer in the baroque era.  Vivaldi was born on 4th March 1678 in the Republic of Venice, today part of Italy; his father was Giovanni Battista, a baker before becoming a professional violinist, who taught his son to play violin.  They subsequently toured Venice playing violin together. Vivaldi suffered from what was called &quot;chest tightening&quot; which might have been asthma; this did not, however, prevent him from learning to play the violin, composing and taking part in the prescribed musical activities.

Roback and Sandoval were the creative center of the band, with Sandoval writing most of the lyrics and Roback composing most of the music.

 START_ARTIST Godspeed You! Black Emperor ::: Montreal, Canada ::: 
                Godspeed You! Black Emperor (formerly punctuated Godspeed You Black Emperor! and abbreviated to GY!BE, GYBE or Godspeed) are a Canadian band based in Montreal, Quebec.   Formed in 1994 in Montreal, Canada, the band has been highly influential within the <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/post-rock" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">post-rock</a> genre. Working with orchestrated arrangements, the nine-piece group created tracks with wide dynamic ranges, a highly evocative use of instrumentation and sounds and uncompromising long form compositions. Their engrossing use of art and visuals in both album packaging and live performances creates an enigmatic aura. 

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Godspeed+You!+Black+Emperor">Read more about Godspeed You! Black Emperor on Last.fm</a>.
    
     END_ARTIST
 START_ARTIST Emilíana Torrini ::: Kópavogur, Iceland ::: 
                Emilíana Torrini (Emilíana Torrini Davíðsdóttir, born on 16 May 1977 in Kópavogur, Iceland) is an <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/Icelandic">Icelandic</a> singer-songwriter, best known for her 2009 single <a title="Emil&iacute;ana Torrini &ndash; Jungle Drum" href="http://www.last.fm/music/Emil%C3%ADana+Torrini/_/Jungle+Drum" class="bbcode_track">Jungle Drum</a>, for  the closing theme entitled <a title="Emil&iacute;ana Torrini &ndash; Gollum's Song" href="http://www.last.fm/music/Emil%C3%ADana+Torrini/_/Gollum%27s+Song" class="bbcode_track">Gollum's Song</a> of &quot;The Lord of the Rings: The Two Towers&quot; film, and for her international debut album, <a title="Emil&iacute;ana Torrini - Love in the Time of Science" href="http://www.last.fm/music/Emil%C3%ADana+Torrini/Love+in+the+Time+of+Science" class="bbcode_album">Love in the Time of Science</a>.  Her father is Italian and her mother Icelandic. Emilíana grew up in Kópavogur where, at the age of 7, she joined a choir as a soprano.  She continued with the choir until she went to opera school at the age of 15.

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Emil%C3%ADana+Torrini">Read more about Emilíana Torrini on Last.fm</a>.

 START_ARTIST ATB ::: Freiberg, Saxony, Germany ::: 
                André Tanneberger aka ATB (born February 26, 1973 in Freiberg, Saxony, Germany) is a DJ, musician, and producer of <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/trance" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">trance</a>, <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/ambient" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">ambient</a> and <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/progressive%20house" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">progressive house</a> music.  Among his most famous songs is “9pm (Till I Come)”, which topped the charts in the United Kingdom in 1998 and is widely regarded as the UK’s first Trance number one. The track features a guitar riff which became hugely popular. This guitar sound, which he accidentally found while experimenting with a new producing deck, became the trademark of his early hits.

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/ATB">Read more about ATB on Last.fm</a>.

 START_ARTIST Chromeo ::: Montreal, Canada and New York City :::

They are <span title="Unknown artist" class="bbcode_unknown">P-Thugg</span> (Patrick Gemayel) on keyboards, synthesizers and talk box, and <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Dave+1" class="bbcode_artist">Dave 1</a> (<a href="http://www.last.fm/music/David+Macklovitch" class="bbcode_artist">David Macklovitch</a>) on guitar and lead vocals.  START_ARTIST Trey Songz ::: Petersburg, Virginia ::: 
                Tremaine Aldon Neverson (born November 28, 1984 in Petersburg, Virginia), better known by his stage name Trey Songz, is a Grammy award nominated American singer, producer and actor. After releasing many mixtapes under the name Prince of Virginia he signed to Atlantic Records in 2005 and released his debut album I Gotta Make It. His second album, Trey Day, was released in 2007 and earned him a Grammy nomination. His latest album, Ready, was released in September 2009 and debuted at #3 on the Billboard 200, and his upcoming album Passion, Pain &amp; Pleasure is expected to be released September 14.

Despite the presence of other heavyweight acts like <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/James+Taylor" class="bbcode_artist">James Taylor</a> and <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Rod+Stewart" class="bbcode_artist">Rod Stewart</a> on their roster, America was Warner Brothers Records' biggest selling act of the 1970s.

 START_ARTIST Roxy Music ::: London, England ::: 
                Roxy Music is a British <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/art%20rock" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">art rock</a> group which formed in 1971 in London, England. Led throughout by <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Bryan+Ferry" class="bbcode_artist">Bryan Ferry</a> (vocals, keyboards), the band attained popular and critical success in Europe and Australia during the 1970s and early 1980s, beginning with their 1972 eponymous debut album. Over its time, the band has been highly influential as leading proponents of the more experimental, musically-sophisticated element of glam-rock, as well as providing a model for many New Wave acts and the experimental electronic groups of the early 1980s.

 START_ARTIST Ace of Base ::: Göteborg, Sweden ::: 
                Swedish <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/pop" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">pop</a> group Ace of Base was formed in Göteborg, Sweden  in 1990.  The band's original lineup consisted of <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Ulf+Ekberg" class="bbcode_artist">Ulf Ekberg</a> (Buddha), and siblings <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Jonas+Berggren" class="bbcode_artist">Jonas Berggren</a> (Joker), <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Linn+Berggren" class="bbcode_artist">Linn Berggren</a> and <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Jenny+Berggren" class="bbcode_artist">Jenny Berggren</a>; the two Berggren sisters left in 2007 and 2009 respectively, and were replaced with  <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Clara+Hagman" class="bbcode_artist">Clara Hagman</a> and <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Julia+Williamson" class="bbcode_artist">Julia Williamson</a>.  Ace Of Base broke through internationally in 1993 with the hit '<a title="Ace of Base &ndash; All That She Wants" href="http://www.last.fm/music/Ace+of+Base/_/All+That+She+Wants" class="bbcode_track">All That She Wants</a>' and one year later with '<a title="Ace of Base &ndash; The Sign" href="http://www.last.fm/music/Ace+of+Base/_/The+Sign" class="bbcode_track">The Sign</a>' worldwide. Their album '<a title="Ace of Base - Happy Nation" href="http://www.last.fm/music/Ace+of+Base/Happy+Nation" class="bbcode_album">Happy Nation</a>' (released as '<a title="Ace of Base - The Sign" href="http://www.last.fm/music/Ace+of+Base/The+Sign" class="bbcode_album">The Sign</a>' in the USA) went on to sell over 20 million copies. 

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Ace+of+Base">Read more about Ace of Base on Last.fm</a>.
    
     END_ARTIST
 START_ARTIST Korpiklaani ::: Lahti, Finland ::: 
                Korpiklaani is a <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/folk%20metal" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">folk metal</a> band from Lahti, Finland formed in 2003. Korpiklaani is the new name of the band previously called <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Shaman" class="bbcode_artist">Shaman</a>, that was formed by Jonne Järvelä who still remains the mastermind of Korpiklaani. Whilst Shaman recorded songs in the original Saami language, Korpiklaani recorded most songs in English at first, and mostly Finnish lyrics on their most recent albums.  The music of Korpiklaani ranges from the violin-and-guitar paean to the Finnish god of fermentation Pellonpekko, to the &quot;typical&quot; themed metal Wooden Pints...

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Korpiklaani">Read more about Korpiklaani on Last.fm</a>.
    
     END_ARTIST
 START_ARTIST Kyuss ::: Palm Desert, California ::: 
                For 2011 touring line-up, see <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Kyuss+Lives!" class="bbcode_artist">Kyuss Lives!</a>.  Kyuss  (pronounced /ˈkaɪ.əs/ KYE-əs) is the corner stone of what is known as <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/stoner%20rock" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">stoner rock</a> or <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/desert%20rock" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">desert rock</a>. Although deriving influence from 60s-70s <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/hard%20rock" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">hard rock</a>, Kyuss churned out a unique sound. This was primarily because guitarist <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Josh+Homme" class="bbcode_artist">Josh Homme</a> often tuned to a low C, a major third below standard pitch, but also singer <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/John+Garcia" class="bbcode_artist">John Garcia</a>'s paint stripping vocals.  The band was originally formed in 1989 in Palm Desert, California under the name &quot;Sons of Kyuss&quot;. They took the name from a monster in Dungeons and Dragons.

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Kyuss">Read more about Kyuss on Last.fm</a>.
    
     END_ARTIST
 START_ARTIST Slash ::: Stoke, England ::: 
                Saul Hudson (born 23 July 1965, Stoke, England), better known by his stage name Slash, is a British-American musician. He is the former lead guitarist of the American Heavy Metal band <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Guns+N%27+Roses" class="bbcode_artist">Guns N' Roses</a>, with whom he performed and recorded between 1985 and 1996. He later formed <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Slash%27s+Snakepit" class="bbcode_artist">Slash's Snakepit</a> and co-founded <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Velvet+Revolver" class="bbcode_artist">Velvet Revolver</a> with his former bandmates <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Duff+McKagan" class="bbcode_artist">Duff McKagan</a> and <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Matt+Sorum" class="bbcode_artist">Matt Sorum</a>; and his debut solo album, <a title="Slash - Slash" href="http://www.last.fm/music/Slash/Slash" class="bbcode_album">Slash</a> , was released in April 2010. In 2011 he wrote and featured on <a title="Slash &ndash; Kick It Up A Notch" href="http://www.last.fm/music/Slash/_/Kick+It+Up+A+Notch" class="bbcode_track">Kick It Up A Notch</a>, the end credit song for The Disney Channel Original Movie Phineas and Ferb: Across the 2nd Dimension.

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Slash">Read more about Slash on Last.fm</a>.
    
     END_ARTIST
 START_ARTIST Amorphis ::: Helsinki, Finland ::: 
                Amorphis is a Finnish <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/progressive%20metal" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">progressive metal</a>, and formerly <span title="Unknown tag" class="bbcode_unknown">Death/Doom</span> band started by Jan Rechberger, Tomi Koivusaari and Esa Holopainen in Helsinki, Finland in 1990. Amorphis absorbed and incorporated influences from many metal genres, and with time passing their sound evolved dramatically. Initially, the band was a <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/death%20metal" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">death metal</a> act, but with time they have evolved into making music that is more classifiable as <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/doom%20metal" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">doom metal</a> with folk influences, and, more recently, <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/progressive%20metal" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">progressive metal</a> and <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/hard%20rock" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">hard rock</a>, utilizing increasingly complex arrangements and a less brutal sound.

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Amorphis">Read more about Amorphis on Last.fm</a>.
    
     END_ARTIST
 START_ARTIST Silverchair ::: Newcastle, New South Wales, Australia ::: 
                Silverchair were one of Australia’s most successful <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/alternative%20rock" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">alternative rock</a> (and formerly <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/post-grunge" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">post-grunge</a>) bands. The group has had more top twenty hits during the last decade than any other local artist and they have sold over six million albums worldwide.  The band formed in 1992 in Newcastle, New South Wales, Australia. In 1994, at the age of 15, Silverchair got their big break when the band won a national competition called &quot;Pick Me&quot; with the demo of their song, &quot;<a title="Silverchair &ndash; Tomorrow" href="http://www.last.fm/music/Silverchair/_/Tomorrow" class="bbcode_track">Tomorrow</a>&quot;.

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Silverchair">Read more about Silverchair on Last.fm</a>.

 START_ARTIST Boys Like Girls ::: Andover, Massachusetts, United States ::: 
                Boys Like Girls is a pop rock band which formed in Andover, Massachusetts, United States in 2005. The band currently consists of Martin Johnson (vocals, guitar), Paul DiGiovanni (guitar, vocals), Morgan Dorr (bass) and John Keefe (drums). The group's original bassist, Bryan Donahue, left the band in 2011.  As of February 2011 the band announced they would be going on an indefinite hiatus. Recently, on November 17th, 2011, Martin Johnson tweeted &quot;...#boyslikegirlsisback&quot;, revealing that the group has not broken up, rather that the members are taking a rest and engaging in various side projects.

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Boys+Like+Girls">Read more about Boys Like Girls on Last.fm</a>.

 START_ARTIST Warpaint ::: Los Angeles, California, United States ::: 
                Warpaint is a psychedelic rock band which formed in 2004 in Los Angeles, California, United States. The band consists of Jenny Lee Lindberg (vocals, bass), Emily Kokal (vocals, guitar), Theresa Wayman (vocals, guitar) and Stella Mozgawa (drums). The band's original drummer, Shannyn Sossamon, left the band in 2008 and was replaced by Mozgawa.  The band weaves intricate guitar lines, hypnotic vocals, and driving post-punk rhythms into gorgeous, sprawling songs that skirt the line between the soundscapes of psychedelia and intimacy.

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Warpaint">Read more about Warpaint on Last.fm</a>.

 START_ARTIST Tinie Tempah ::: London ::: 
                Patrick Junior C. Okogwu (born November 7th, 1988 in Plumstead, South London), better known by his stage name Tinie Tempah, is a BRIT Award-winning rapper, MC and CEO of Disturbing London Records. Tinie gained national acclaim and chart success upon the release of his major label debut single <a title="Tinie Tempah &ndash; Pass Out" href="http://www.last.fm/music/Tinie+Tempah/_/Pass+Out" class="bbcode_track">Pass Out</a> which debuted at #1 on the UK Singles Chart in March 2010.  According to the <a href="http://www.songfacts.com/detail.php?id=18441" rel="nofollow">Pass Out Songfacts</a>, Okogwu came up with his stage name at the age of 13. He looked up 'anger' in the thesaurus and found himself staring at 'temper.' Concerned it might be overly aggresive he added 'Tinie.' 

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Tinie+Tempah">Read more about Tinie Tempah on Last.fm</a>.
    
     END_ARTIST
 START_ARTIST 311 ::: Omaha, Nebraska, United States ::: 
                311 was formed in 1990 in Omaha, Nebraska, United States by singer/guitarist Nick Hexum, singer S.A. Martinez, guitarist Tim Mahoney, drummer Chad Sexton and bassist P-Nut. The band now resides in Los Angeles, California.
  
 311 mix rock, rap, reggae and funk into their own unique sound. After years of consistent touring, 311 have developed a reputation as one of the hardest working, most influential and most entertaining live bands in the U.S.
  
 

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/311">Read more about 311 on Last.fm</a>.

 START_ARTIST Meshuggah ::: Umeå, Sweden ::: 
                Meshuggah, whose name is taken from the Hebrew and Yiddish word for “crazy”, is a five-piece band from Umeå, Sweden, founded in 1987. The band's style is most easily described as <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/extreme" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">extreme</a>/<a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/technical%20metal" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">technical metal</a> with some <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/jazz" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">jazz</a> influence. They use extended polymetric passages, polyrhythmic drum patterns, angular, dissonant guitar riffs, and harsh vocals. Their lineup has always been consistent, apart from bass which has been handled by many people since the band’s inception.

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Meshuggah">Read more about Meshuggah on Last.fm</a>.

 START_ARTIST Dashboard Confessional ::: Boca Raton, Florida ::: 
                Dashboard Confessional was started in 2000, by <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Chris+Carrabba" class="bbcode_artist">Chris Carrabba</a> in Boca Raton, Florida, as a side project from his band <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Further+Seems+Forever" class="bbcode_artist">Further Seems Forever</a>.  Chris recorded his first album, The Swiss Army Romance, in 2000. The following year, he recorded Further Seems Forever's debut album The Moon Is Down. However, he left the band soon after the album's release, instead recording and releasing his sophomore album The Places You Have Come to Fear the Most, as well as a follow-up EP titled So Impossible.

                Rufus McGarrigle Wainwright (born 22 July 1973) is a <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/canadian">Canadian</a>-<a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/american">American</a> <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/singer-songwriter" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">singer-songwriter</a>.  START_ARTIST George Harrison ::: Liverpool, UK ::: 
                George Harrison, MBE (25 February 1943 – 29 November 2001) born in Liverpool, UK, was an English rock musician, singer-songwriter and film producer who achieved international fame as lead guitarist in <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/The+Beatles" class="bbcode_artist">The Beatles</a>, along with mainstream success as a solo artist. George contributed to the songwriting talents of his Beatles band mates, <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/John+Lennon" class="bbcode_artist">John Lennon</a> and <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Paul+McCartney" class="bbcode_artist">Paul McCartney</a>, firstly by adding ideas and guitar parts, and later with his distinctive style of music inspired by Eastern spirituality.

 START_ARTIST Elvis Costello ::: London ::: 
                Elvis Costello (born Declan Patrick MacManus on 25 August 1954) is an English singer-songwriter. He came to prominence as an early participant in London's pub rock scene in the mid-1970s and soon became associated with the punk/New Wave genre (as <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Elvis+Costello+&amp;+The+Attractions" class="bbcode_artist">Elvis Costello &amp; The Attractions</a>). In a long and successful career, Costello has released over 30 studio albums on his own and with the Attractions, the Imposters, and other collaborations.

 START_ARTIST Alien Ant Farm ::: Riverside, California, United States ::: 
                Alien Ant Farm is an alternative rock/metal band which formed in 1995 in Riverside, California, United States. The band consists of Dryden Mitchell (vocals, guitar), Terry Corso (guitar), Tye Zamora (bass) and Mike Cosgrove (drums). They are best known for their 2001 cover of Michael Jackson's &quot;Smooth Criminal&quot; and the follow up hits &quot;Movies&quot; and &quot;These Days&quot;. It went on to win Best Independent Album in the L.A. Music Awards.

 START_ARTIST The Zombies ::: St Albans, England ::: 
                The Zombies were a pop rock/psychedelic rock band that formed in 1961 in St Albans, England and gained their initial reputation playing the Old Verulamians Rugby Club in that town. The group was formed whilst the members, <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Rod+Argent" class="bbcode_artist">Rod Argent</a>, <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Paul+Atkinson" class="bbcode_artist">Paul Atkinson</a> and <span title="Unknown artist" class="bbcode_unknown">Hugh Grundy</span> attended St Albans School and <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Colin+Blunstone" class="bbcode_artist">Colin Blunstone</a> and <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Chris+White" class="bbcode_artist">Chris White</a> were at St Albans Boys' Grammar School.   The Zombies signed to Decca and recorded their first hit, &quot;She's Not There&quot; after winning a beat-group competition sponsored by the London Evening News.

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/The+Zombies">Read more about The Zombies on Last.fm</a>.

In 2005, Tokyo Police Club started by accident one day in the ordinary suburb of Newmarket when Greg, Josh, Dave, and Graham decided that they missed playing music together, their previous band having broken up several months before.

 START_ARTIST King Crimson ::: London, England, United Kingdom ::: 
                King Crimson were a progressive rock group from London, England, United Kingdom formed in 1968 by guitarist <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Robert+Fripp" class="bbcode_artist">Robert Fripp</a> and drummer <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Michael+Giles" class="bbcode_artist">Michael Giles</a>. Though originally an all-British musical group, later members have included a number of Americans, most notably <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Adrian+Belew" class="bbcode_artist">Adrian Belew</a>, and <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Tony+Levin" class="bbcode_artist">Tony Levin</a>.  The name &quot;King Crimson&quot; was coined by <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Peter+Sinfield" class="bbcode_artist">Peter Sinfield</a> as a synonym for Beelzebub, prince of demons.  King Crimson's debut album was <a title="King Crimson - In the Court of the Crimson King" href="http://www.last.fm/music/King+Crimson/In+the+Court+of+the+Crimson+King" class="bbcode_album">In the Court of the Crimson King</a>.

 START_ARTIST Buffalo Springfield ::: Los Angeles, California, United States ::: 
                Buffalo Springfield are a <a href="http://www.last.fm/tag/folk%20rock" class="bbcode_tag" rel="tag">folk rock</a> band which formed in 1966 in Los Angeles, California, United States. The band's original lineup consisted of <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Neil+Young" class="bbcode_artist">Neil Young</a> (vocals, guitar), <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Stephen+Stills" class="bbcode_artist">Stephen Stills</a> (vocals, guitar), <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Richie+Furay" class="bbcode_artist">Richie Furay</a> (vocals, guitar), <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Bruce+Palmer" class="bbcode_artist">Bruce Palmer</a>  (bass) and Dewey Martin (drums). Palmer left the band in 1968 and was replaced by <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Jim+Messina" class="bbcode_artist">Jim Messina</a>. The band's only Top 40 single, &quot;<a title="Buffalo Springfield &ndash; For What It's Worth" href="http://www.last.fm/music/Buffalo+Springfield/_/For+What+It%27s+Worth" class="bbcode_track">For What It's Worth</a>&quot;, was released in 1967. The band split in 1968.

        <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Buffalo+Springfield">Read more about Buffalo Springfield on Last.fm</a>.
